<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:еле.html>е́ле</a> (1774)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:еле.html>е́ле</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jéle</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hardly, scarcely, barely</li>
<li>slightly</li>
<li>with (great) difficulty</li></ol>

<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔλαιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">élaion</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">oil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ель.html>еле́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jeléj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:елей.html>еле́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:елей.html>еле́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:елей.html>еле́ев</a></b>)

<ol><li>holy oil, chrism</li>

***елисейский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:елисейский.html>елисе́йский</a> (23902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">эли́сий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Elísij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Elysium</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">эли́сий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Elísij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is a less common form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">эли́зий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Elízij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">эли́зиум</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Elízium</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The former term was borrowed directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Ἠλύσιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Ēlúsion</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Elysian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, while the latter two terms came via Latin, in turn from the same Greek word.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:елисейский.html>елисе́йский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jeliséjskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Elysian, paradisiacal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:елисейский.html>елисе́йские</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поле.html>поля́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jeliséjskije</b> poljá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Champs-%C3%89lys%C3%A9es" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Champs-Élysées">Champs-Élysées</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">famous avenue in Paris</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">эли́сий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Elísij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">эли́зий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Elízij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">эли́зиум</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Elízium</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***елозить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:елозить.html>ело́зить</a> (21423)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">елоза́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jelozá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fidgety person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of unclear further provenance.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:елозить.html>ело́зить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jelózitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to crawl</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fidget</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move randomly and constantly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of one's fingers, elbows, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move around in different directions <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, something, e.g. a toothbrush in one's mouth, a bow on violin strings, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***ель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ель.html>ель</a> (14922)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*edlь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ель.html>ель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:есть.html>е́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:есть.html>е́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ель.html>е́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spruce</li>
<li>fir-tree</li></ol>

***емкость.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:емкость.html>ёмкость</a> (8274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:емкий.html>ёмкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jómkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:емкость.html>ёмкость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jómkostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:емкость.html>ёмкости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:емкость.html>ёмкости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:емкость.html>ёмкостей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>capacitance, capacity, volume</li>
<li>bottle, or anything that can hold liquid, usually of higher capacity
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пусту́ю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:емкость.html>ёмкость</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:налить.html>нали́ли</a> 40 (<a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>со́рок</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:литр.html>ли́тров</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V pustúju <b>jómkostʹ</b> nalíli 40 (sórok) lítrov vodý.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(Someone) poured 40 liters of water into the empty bottle.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">electronics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> capacitor</li></ol>

***енот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:енот.html>ено́т</a> (19500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Genette</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">genette</i>, with unclear -<i><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></i>-. The original meaning was “genet”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:енот.html>ено́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jenót</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:енот.html>ено́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:енот.html>ено́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:енот.html>ено́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> genet</li>

***епархия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:епархия.html>епа́рхия</a> (29311)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:епархия.html>епа́рхия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jepárxija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:епархия.html>епа́рхии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:епархия.html>епа́рхии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:епархия.html>епа́рхий</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">епархиа́льный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>diocese, bishopric</li>
<li>domain, sphere of competence, area of responsibility
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:епархия.html>епа́рхия</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto uže ne mojá <b>jepárxija</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">it's outside my province</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ерунда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ерунда.html>ерунда́</a> (3347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ерунда.html>ерунда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jerundá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ерунда.html>ерунды́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> sometimes derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nonsense, rubbish</li>
<li>trifle</li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:ротмистр.html>ро́тмистр</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:капитан.html>капита́н</a></li></ol>
</body> 
***если.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> (51)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">li</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Appeared in the 16th-17th centuries in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ruthenian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ruthenian language">Western Russian</a>, likely as a result of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">jeśli</i> influence<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jésli</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>if, in case
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кино.html>кино́</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja by pošól v kinó, <b>jésli</b> by u menjá býlo vrémja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I would have gone to the cinema if I had had time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">a <b>jésli</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">if ever</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jésli</b> i</i> ― <span class="e-translation">even though</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jésli</b> tólʹko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">provided</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:естество.html>естество́</a> (19165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">there is</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ество́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-estvó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:естество.html>естество́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jestestvó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:естество.html>естества́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>nature, essence</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***есть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> (73)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ěsti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*ēˀstei</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁édti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jestʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:съесть.html>съесть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поесть.html>пое́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to eat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> поедо́м</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jestʹ pojedóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make somebody's life a misery by nagging</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прое́сться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">projéstʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разъе́сть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razʺjéstʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разъе́сться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razʺjéstʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jestʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present indicative of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>there is, there are, exists/exist <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">expresses availability, existence or presence</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">net</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:газета.html>газе́те</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:интересный.html>интере́сная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:статья.html>статья́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v étoj gazéte <b>jestʹ</b> interésnaja statʹjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is an interesting article in this newspaper</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>am/is/are located (at) (usually omitted)</li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">used to express possession</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u menjá <b>jestʹ</b> voprós</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have a question</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>am, is, are (used with any person or thing in any number, usually omitted but used for emphasis)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kto ty <b>jestʹ</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">who are you (at all)?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is special and most frequently used in the present tense, for past and future tense and other forms, see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>The pre-reform orthography (1918) form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ѣсть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jěstʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> doesn't apply to this sense, only to the sense "to eat", thus the two terms were spelled differently before the reform.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">yes</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jestʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>all right</li>
<li>okay, right, roger</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yessir!</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> aye-aye!</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ефрейтор.html>ефре́йтор</a> (6634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gefreiter</i> with the dialectal realization <span class="IPA">/j/</span> for word-initial ‹g› found in many Central German dialects including large parts of historical Prussia.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ефрейтор.html>ефре́йтор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jefréjtor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ефрейтор.html>ефре́йтора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ефрейтор.html>ефре́йторы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ефрейтор.html>ефре́йторов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lance corporal <i>(military rank)</i></li></ol>

***ехать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a> (460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ěxati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jéxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хать</a></b>) <i>(concrete)</i>
</p>
<ol><li>to go (by horse or vehicle), to ride, to drive</li>
<li>to travel</li>
<li>to move from a place, to slide off</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>Е́хать</a></b> and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pojéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jézditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is an abstract verb.</li>
<li>The imperative forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">едь</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jedʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">е́дьте</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jédʹte</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">е́хай</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jéxaj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">е́хайте</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jéxajte</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (including derivatives with prefixes) are used but are considered illiterate and are not recommended for use. The recommended imperative forms are suppletive forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>поезжа́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pojezžáj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>поезжа́йте</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pojezžájte</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> but <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>езжа́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jezžáj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>езжа́йте</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jezžájte</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are also acceptable. The derivatives (<a href = vnd.unilang:приезжать.html>приезжа́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:заезжать.html>заезжа́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:выезжать.html>выезжа́ть</a>, etc.) use prefix + <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>езжа́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jezžáj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / prefix + <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>езжа́йте</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jezžájte</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>The present adverbial form <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́дучи</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jéduči</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is dated.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i>See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jézditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for derived verbs.</i></li></ul>

***ехидный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехидный.html>ехи́дный</a> (17673)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ехи́д(<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jexíd(na)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***ея.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ея</a> (31604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ея́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jejá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reforms_of_Russian_orthography" class="extiw" title="w:Reforms of Russian orthography">Pre-1918 spelling</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jejó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>. <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the possessive pronoun, and of the genitive of personal pronoun</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This was usually pronounced the same as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jejó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which was also the spelling of the accusative of personal pronoun.</li></ul>

***ж.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a> (293)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Letter_4">Letter</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ž</span>) (<i>lower case</i>, <i>upper case</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>Ж</a></b>) (<i>italics: <a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>Ж</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The eighth letter of the Russian Cyrillic alphabet.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Its name is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">že</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and it sounds like the <b>s</b> in <i>plea<b>s</b>ure</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ž</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Apocopic form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">že</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Abbreviation of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žénskij rod</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">feminine gender</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a>.</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ž.</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жабра.html>жа́бра</a> (23262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">жа́бри</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žábry</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">же́бры</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žjébry</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">жа́бри</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žábri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">žábra</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">žiabra</i>, but a Proto-Slavic form hasn't been reconstructed.
